        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582346405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18308386948622236270">Well Damn! When you think that Nalini Singh couldn't possibly have done it again she goes all the way to prove you wrong. I mean...WOW!!!(Eloquent I know.)<br/><br/>I have just one question for my very best author.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384163572ra/6799092.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What can I say about this book without spoiling it? When Aly told me that this one was as good as Angels' Blood I wasn't so optimistic but this one was quite possibly better. I think this is officially my new favorite in the series and that says a lot since I absolutely LOVE the first one.<br/><br/>In thi</span>
  <span id="freeText18308386948622236270" style="display:none">Well Damn! When you think that Nalini Singh couldn't possibly have done it again she goes all the way to prove you wrong. I mean...WOW!!!(Eloquent I know.)<br><br>I have just one question for my very best author.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384163572ra/6799092.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say about this book without spoiling it? When Aly told me that this one was as good as Angels' Blood I wasn't so optimistic but this one was quite possibly better. I think this is officially my new favorite in the series and that says a lot since I absolutely LOVE the first one.<br><br>In this book Raphael and Elena(and the New York angels in general) don't seem to be able to catch a break. Danger after danger seem to threaten their lives and peace. When angels start falling from the sky and vamps to die from a mysterious disease when they should have been immune to any kind of virus our favorite couple knows they are in trouble. What happens next is in one word Epic. Nalini Singh managed to twist the story again and again without making you a mess, trying to figure out what happened.<br><br>The very best thing in this book was the dynamics in Raphael's and Elena's relationship. Since the beginning of their entanglement Raphael always seemed to be the one making the decisions, the one with all the cards. In AL we finally see a true partnership. He asks for her opinion, capitulates to some of her wishes, includes her in the decisions. It was great to read this. <br><br>Elena also grows up during the book a lot. Her headstrong ways don't change much but she begins to realise that in a world ruled by politics sometimes you need to think before you act. Btw I found really cute the fact that Elena was jealous. We have seen her get a pissy eye with Michaela but it never was exactly jealousy, she is just a bitch and Elena hates her but isn't really jealous of her and Raphael. Actually seeing Elena jealous was fun.<br><br>The other past of the book that I loved was Aodhan. He is rapidly rising in my list of favorites in the series. For now he is up there with Ilium, Venom and Naasir, because I really can't choose between them. I wanted his book to be the next, instead I get Ash and Javier. I have to admit that although I want to know what happens with them I'd have prefered it to be a novella instead of a full length book.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I can't wait to see what the Primary will evolve into after the Legion's people separate. God, what a twist. I know we'll be seeing more of him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384163572i/6799093._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384163572ra/6799094.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can't wait for what Nalini has in mind for us next.<br><br><b>****************14/04/2014****************</b><br><br>I had two points I wanted to mention after my re-read. I even had them written down. Too bad I wrote them on a post-it that I lost. I really don't remember page numbers or what exactly it was that I wanted to include.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397500235ra/9283990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know it wasn't negative though...:P</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="18308386948622236270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2980748178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8128221676654938560">I had thought book 5 lacked a bit of action and let's just say, book 6 made up for that. That extra action at the end just made me love this couple even more. The love that Raphael and Elena have for each other is really felt on the pages. My favorite thing to read about is a couple who are totally devoted to each other and won't allow anyone or anything to come in between them. You get that with these two. I also like that with this being book 6, I'm in no way bored with this series. It's still</span>
  <span id="freeText8128221676654938560" style="display:none">I had thought book 5 lacked a bit of action and let's just say, book 6 made up for that. That extra action at the end just made me love this couple even more. The love that Raphael and Elena have for each other is really felt on the pages. My favorite thing to read about is a couple who are totally devoted to each other and won't allow anyone or anything to come in between them. You get that with these two. I also like that with this being book 6, I'm in no way bored with this series. It's still just as exciting as book 1. There is a lot going on that keeps your attention and many things still to be revealed about this world. On to book 7!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8128221676654938560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4030071821198093994"><b> Amazing! Absolutely blew my mind!</b><br/><br/>Every time I read one of her books, I'm constantly struck by Nalini's Singh capability in totally capturing your attention with the story that she weaves! I love it, absolutely adore her writing.<br/>The world she'd built in Guild Hunter series is unforgettable.<br/>She's one of the authors I follow, hopping she'll release new books.<br/><br/>This book was.. huh..   <span id="freeText4030071821198093994" style="display:none"><b> Amazing! Absolutely blew my mind!</b><br /><br />Every time I read one of her books, I'm constantly struck by Nalini's Singh capability in totally capturing your attention with the story that she weaves! I love it, absolutely adore her writing.<br />The world she'd built in Guild Hunter series is unforgettable.<br />She's one of the authors I follow, hopping she'll release new books.<br /><br />This book was.. huh.. I'm actually a little bit speechless after everything that I just read. Raw emotions still fights within me. Goddammit I was scared for a minute there.. But worry not my dear fellow readers. The ending was epic and beautiful. And it was totally worth the wait of my paperback to arrive. I'm usually less patient and just buy a kindle version. But to really touch what she wrote was beyond ecstatic! <br /><br />So do us all a favor and read this series if you haven't yet. No, that came out wrong. Do Yourself a favor and READ THIS SERIES! <br />Cause it's like a day at the spa! Her writing takes you to a whole new level of ecstasy! <br />After so many poorly written books that I've read, it's a relaxation beyond all. I've noticed this some time ago, when I was reading Psy-Changeling series back to back. No matter how intense the action, or how many events went wrong in the book, I was still pleased. The writing is that good!<br /><br />enough of my rambling.<br /><br />Go, GO! Go read Archangel's Legion!<br /><br /><br />Peace,<br />A.</span>

<div id="review_1795604573" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1795604573" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1795604573?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575112148" href="/book/show/18163825-archangel-s-legion">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1795604573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16350107387050200833"><b>1st read: November 2013</b><br/><b>2nd read: October 2016</b><br/><b>3rd read: September 2020</b><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>It's no secret that I've become a bit of a <b>Nalini Singh</b> fan girl since I discovered the Guild Hunter series, I'm slowly working my way through her Psy-Changeling books too and really enjoying them but Raphael and Elena will always have a special place in my heart. Because I'm such a huge fan I always have very high expectations when I pick up a new <b>Nalini Singh</b> book and I'm always slightly nervous that I've built</span>
  <span id="freeText16350107387050200833" style="display:none"><b>1st read: November 2013</b><br /><b>2nd read: October 2016</b><br /><b>3rd read: September 2020</b><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />It's no secret that I've become a bit of a <b>Nalini Singh</b> fan girl since I discovered the Guild Hunter series, I'm slowly working my way through her Psy-Changeling books too and really enjoying them but Raphael and Elena will always have a special place in my heart. Because I'm such a huge fan I always have very high expectations when I pick up a new <b>Nalini Singh</b> book and I'm always slightly nervous that I've built the series up so much in my memory that it can't possibly live up to them. Thankfully NS never fails to not just meet but completely surpass my expectations though and with every single book she just makes me love her writing more.<br /><br />It's been a while since we had a book where Raphael and Elena were the main players and as much as I've enjoyed getting to know some of the other characters in the series I was incredibly excited to go back to my favourites. I adore everything about this couple, the way they have changed and grown together throughout the series has been incredible to watch. They still have their issues but I love that they always put each other first, they are aware of their own insecurities and personal issues, they know each other's triggers and most importantly they are willing to put in the effort needed to make a success of their relationship. They don't always agree with each other but they talk things through and even Raphael has learnt to compromise in certain situations. Elena and Raphael are both so much stronger together than they ever could be apart and their relationship is incredibly swoon worthy. I honestly think I could read 100 different books about them and not get bored!<br /><br />As if spending time with Raphael and Elena wasn't enough we also get some incredibly poignant moments between Illium and Aodhan, ones that will bring happy tears to your eyes and make you even more desperate to read their stories. I'm also incredibly curious about Naasir after getting to know a bit more about him. All of Raphael's seven have a major part to play in this one along with Elena's fellow Guild Hunters so we get to catch up with a lot of familiar faces - I have no idea how <b>Nalini Singh</b> manages to pack so much into her stories but she does it like an expert. There are some epic fight scenes that are described so well it's almost like watching a movie (boy would I love to see this series on the big screen!) and the action is pretty much non-stop throughout.<br /><br />I really don't want to say much about the plot because I think you're much better off going in knowing as little as possible to make the most of the experience. What I will say is that <b>Archangel's Legion</b> is a completely and utterly addictive read, it will break your heart, it will make you laugh out loud, you'll be shocked, horrified, angry and upset one minute then ecstatically happy and swooning the next. One thing you won't be able to do is put the book down for a single second so clear your diary before you start reading! This book is a game changer in terms of the series, it opens up so many possibilities that I can't even guess at where <b>Nalini Singh</b> is planning on taking us next but I do know it'll be one hell of an adventure. I think I'd have to say that <b>Archangel's Legion</b> is now my favourite instalment of the series and that's saying something considering how much I've loved the previous books. I honestly can't recommend this series highly enough to paranormal romance and urban fantasy fans, it really is essential reading!<br /><br />________________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />I'd forgotten so much about what happened in this book, there's just so many awesome things going on and I loved being back with Elena and Raphael. As much as I've enjoyed seeing more of the world and getting to know some of the secondary characters I just love spending time with these two and I really enjoy seeing the progression in their relationship. They both have to work at opening up with each other and putting their pasts behind them so things aren't perfect between them but they trust each other implicitly and they understand each other better than they understand themselves half the time.<br /><br />It's the moments between Aodhan and Illium that really made me melt though, I've shipped those two for such a long time now but I'm seeing lots more hints of a potential relationship between them this time around than I ever did before. I'm not sure if it's just wishful thinking but I'm going to be very disappointed if they end up with other people LOL.<br /><br />I loved this series from the very first book but I'm enjoying it even more the second time around and I can't wait to reread the rest!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16350107387050200833" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/522286175?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522286175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12954578358458000858"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2013/11/arc-review-giveaway-archangels-legion-by-nalini-singh.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>4.5 stars, Top Pick!<br/><br/>Queen of Paranormal Romance, Nalini Singh returns to the Guild Hunter series with Elena and Raphael. The sole reason why I fell in love with this series in the first place was because of this couple. I loved Raphael as a hero because he was this god-like creature whose power is unparalleled in the world he has created. But in the first book, we saw him succumb to a more human emotion that makes him more endearing and real: love.<br/><br/>Raphael undergoes a few changes in this late</span>
  <span id="freeText12954578358458000858" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2013/11/arc-review-giveaway-archangels-legion-by-nalini-singh.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>4.5 stars, Top Pick!<br><br>Queen of Paranormal Romance, Nalini Singh returns to the Guild Hunter series with Elena and Raphael. The sole reason why I fell in love with this series in the first place was because of this couple. I loved Raphael as a hero because he was this god-like creature whose power is unparalleled in the world he has created. But in the first book, we saw him succumb to a more human emotion that makes him more endearing and real: love.<br><br>Raphael undergoes a few changes in this latest installment. When birds and angels begin to drop from the sky for the duration of five horrific minutes, New York is put into a state of panic as they try to find out what happened and deal with the number of deaths this has caused. Elena, with the help of her friends, Ransom, Sara and even Deacon try to find out what it is that has caused what they call The Falling.<br><br>The threat becomes more dire when Raphael bears an unidentified mark on his face that is slowly spreading. Could it be linked to the infection that is trolling the city? Furthermore, the all-powerful Raphael is hearing voices in his sleep, a symptom of madness that his father once had as well. Who are the voices he hears and does this mean that the Archangel of New York is swirling into madness?<br><br>Elena’s character has always been relatable in this series, but I feel that is amplified more in this book. We’ve learned of her tragic past and how Slater ruined her life and took those of her mother and sisters. But this time, we get more detail about the event and Elena’s reactions to that kind of loss. We also see her relationship with her father and how grief still remains as a heavy blanket over them even years later.<br><br>The politics once again come into play. With Lijuan and her army becoming a threat again and Raphael’s mother, Caliane stirring up more trouble when she declares that there will never be easiness between her and Lijuan, tension mounts until the threat of war soon becomes an issue.<br><br>What I love about this series is the lush descriptions that paint out the whole scenery in my mind. This world in my mind is so clear and vivid because of Singh’s attention to detail. While not my favorite of Elena and Raphael’s books, ARCHANGEL’S LEGION is a solid installment to the series. It addresses the darkest elements of Elena and Raphael’s most greatest fears and tackles them, making for incredible character development and just a wonderful story.<br><br>If you haven’t already read this series, then I highly suggest you do. It still remains as one of my favorites.<br><br>*ARC provided by publisher</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1798012158" />
    <a title="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3481302-eon-windrunner"><img alt="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551272804p2/3481302.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1798012158?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eon ♒Windrunner♒  " href="/user/show/3481302-eon-windrunner">Eon ♒Windrunner♒  </a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1798012158" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12976121044785730558">4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Now <b>
  <i>this</i>
</b> is how every book in this series should be. <br/><br/>Angels are affected by some unknown force and start falling form the skies, and soon after, vampires, heretofore immune to the ravages of disease are succumbing to a mysterious but rapid-killing illness. Is the Cascade or the first shot from one of their enemies? Raphael & Elena have their hands full with solving these mysteries and stopping the disease from becoming a full blown pandemic. And then Lijuan, the archangel of death, </span>
  <span id="freeText12976121044785730558" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br />Now <b>
  <i>this</i>
</b> is how every book in this series should be. <br /><br />Angels are affected by some unknown force and start falling form the skies, and soon after, vampires, heretofore immune to the ravages of disease are succumbing to a mysterious but rapid-killing illness. Is the Cascade or the first shot from one of their enemies? Raphael &amp; Elena have their hands full with solving these mysteries and stopping the disease from becoming a full blown pandemic. And then Lijuan, the archangel of death, declares war upon Raphael, the only archangel apart from his mother powerful enough to have a hope of defeating her.<br /><br />Good times.<br /><br />The book was great, very entertaining and Nalini Singh has kept up the thorough worldbuilding, excellent characters and engaging storyline. The relationships as before are a focus point with the deeper look at the progress Raphael and Elena have made as a couple being a highlight in this regard. Do not make the mistake of thinking the author skimped on the action though. The story features a massive &amp; deadly battle filled with angels, vampires, zombies, other supernatural forces and…butterflies. ;)<br /><br />The best of the bunch so far and I can only hope the rest of the series matches or surpasses this one.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12976121044785730558" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_520498210" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/520498210" />
    <a title="Ren Puspita" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3666031-ren-puspita"><img alt="Ren Puspita" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531111155p2/3666031.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/520498210?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ren Puspita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ren Puspita" href="/user/show/3666031-ren-puspita">Ren Puspita</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=top-read-2013">top-read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=drooling-cover">drooling-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=own-and-reread">own-and-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=own-mass-market">own-mass-market</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=abused-character">abused-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=immortal-warrior">immortal-warrior</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520498210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11448932415753590315"><b>RE-READ in order to read Archangel's Prophecy and Archangel's War. </b><br/><br/>And also part of my Guild Hunter series read-a-thon, in which I decide to become hermit at my home in this weekend just so I can read my book in peace. Heh, sorry..not sorry :P<br/><br/>I won't write longer re-read review because the original review below already summed up my experience and re-read still not change that, hahaha. Things that I notice are, that even Raphael and Elena get their happy end, nah, the problem didn't end. Both sti</span>
  <span id="freeText11448932415753590315" style="display:none"><b>RE-READ in order to read Archangel's Prophecy and Archangel's War. </b><br /><br />And also part of my Guild Hunter series read-a-thon, in which I decide to become hermit at my home in this weekend just so I can read my book in peace. Heh, sorry..not sorry :P<br /><br />I won't write longer re-read review because the original review below already summed up my experience and re-read still not change that, hahaha. Things that I notice are, that even Raphael and Elena get their happy end, nah, the problem didn't end. Both still have to work their differences, some are fundamentals that threaten to tear them apart if they are not careful. But that's why I like this pairing. Not all are happy rainbows and sunshine, since they still have so many things to learn. Also... I like the angry sex scenes. Sigh, no fighting between lover is complete with angry sex that follow afterward :P. <br /><br />Anyway, I like the way Singh handle about Tasha McHotpants (Elena's term, not mine, lol). Singh handle it with care without make Elena seems vindictive. With a being that immortal like Raphael, of course there's will be an ex. But seems like there general consensus from reader that dislike Tasha. Lol, I agree with it, tho. Oh, and one more, the battle part is my favorite too! I like the description of the war event and glad, even there's some deus ex machinae plot, it's just subtly written in a way that won't annoyed the hell of me.<br /><br />Aaaand...the re-read review already get this long. Sorryyyy...! :P<br /><br />Sigh, I want to re-read Legion again, and despite I said Archangel's Kiss is my favorite Guild Hunter book to date, I loved Archangel's Legion more. It's just perfect like what I had stated below. I almost afraid that Archangel's Prophecy and Archangel's War will not hold my expectation, but I guess I must lower my expectation and just enjoy the book (I did remember that Archangel's Heart, while still a good book, didn't make a lasting impression like this one. I might be wrong after I do re-read tho). Yes, the temptation to re-read again is so great, but I still have many books left to read! Oh, the agony! <br /><br />First reading review below:<br /><br /><b>5 Awesomeness stars and Top Read 2013!!</b><br /><br />Nalini Singh is one of my favorite authors that I always anticipated what next come from her. Her writing style is fabulous, the plot and world she create is beyond amazing, and you can't help to awe for how she can weave words after words that so beautiful, you can't help to not read it over and over! I always love her Guild Hunter more than Psy Changeling series. Both Elena and Raphael are my favorite couple and I'm soooo happy when knowing Archangel's Legion back to them again. It's not that I'm not enjoyed Dmitri's and Jason's, but what make me adore Guild Hunter, beside the world and the story, is come from Elena and Raphael's relationship.<br /><br />In this new installment of the Guild Hunter, Elena and Raphael once again face threat for their territory. Elena also got her hands full, act as consort, a Hunter, also a sister for her half little sister, Eve, a hunter like her, much to Jeffrey's dismay. I'm so sad when reading about Elena and Jeffrey's relationship. I can't help to not sympathize toward Marguerite, Elena's mother to left them both. To make them hurt beyond compare. But, there's maybe hope for Elena and Jeffrey to finally make amend. It's just not now.<br /><br /><blockquote><b><i>Elena shook her head, gripping her mother's wrist in a futile effort to hold her to the world. "He hates me".<br /><br />"No, Elena. He loves you too much."</i></b> </blockquote><br /><br />There are trouble in paradise for both Elena and Raphael. First, Raphael seems like develop some strange power that make Elena so worried. But turn that the power is sooooo awesome. I mean, he can struck lightning, and the scene when he do that? One word. <b>Orgasm</b><br /><br /><blockquote><b><i>Shoving Elena behind him so she wouldn't unbalance and fall, he rose into the sky, high above the clouds, past where even Illium or Aodhan could fly. </i>Land!<i>It was an order blasted out to every angel in the vicinity.<br /><br />Then, and with only the slighest hesitation at the loss of the profound violence of power, he released the dark matter of it in a lightning storm that cracked the sky</i></b> </blockquote><br /><br />It's soooo awesooome, right? I can't even... *sigh*<br /><br />And, it's not enough that Elena must face Michaela, aka the Bitch Goddess (who seems attempt to infiltrate Raphael's territory again by say that she is pregnant. But we know how cunning Michaela is!), not forget that Caliane, Raphael's one mofo Mom still not welcome Elena, now there's a lover from Raphael's past. While Tasha is a warrior of her own, Elena do has right to despise her since Tasha seems to want Raphael by herself. Poor Elena, but then she never back off from anything that will treat her love for Raphael. And I'm glad that Tasha is not bitchy like Michaela. Just one is enough, imho.<br /><br />After we got "almost war scene" in the previous books, finally in Archangel's Legion, the war happen. It's not spoiler, if you already read the 3 first books, readers will know that Raphael must face Lijuan. And the war part, right now doesn't disappoint me. It's grand, gory and full of tactics. There's also a hopeless feeling from Raphael, that he can't defend Manhattan from Lijuan's attack. And while another Archangels more like behind the scene, I wonder if they will make more appearance in the next books. The alliance of The Cadre already forged, and who's know that finally Raphael will be the strongest of them all?<br /><br />After he shut himself for eternity, it's like that Aodhan become the attention for Archangel's Legion, for he finally decide to open to other. I know that some readers want Aodhan and Illium have something more in their relationship, but I'm with Nalini in this. Why can they remain be friends, a close friend who have each other back, much like Raphael and Dmitri? If they will become like lover, I'm afraid it will be forced. So I'm totally agree with "bromance" part. Naasir, well, finally he got so much scene, for he is "other" than another vampires in Seven. I wonder what he is, or if he truly a vampire at all. Sadly, not so much for Venom and Galen, since they must defend the Refuge. And just a little from Jason and Dmitri<br /><br />Elena and Raphael, ahh.. where I can start? They have some rocky moments, of course. But it's so wonderful to know how they work into their difference. Their sex scene are steamy and plenty! Alas, there's no "angel dance" for I want to read it again. Guess I will re-read Archangel's Consort after this ;).<br /><br />Nalini's writing is superb, and as I write this review, I kinda have a book hangover! I don't know what to read next. What I want is to read Archangel's Legion again and again. I wait for this book to come in month, and the wait is totally worth it! I'm so sad to know that the next book is about Ashwini and Janvier, for I want to read about Elena and Raphael again. They're still have so much problem to solved after all.<br /><br />Archangel's Legion is one of my favorite read this year. It's not absolute perfect of course (Nalini kinda have habit to repeat some part over and over. Like how Elena will not let Raphael down, if he consume by madness. And the nightmare), but I still love it nonetheless. If only Nalini Singh can write faster :')<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You know what I've learned from my baby girl? To enjoy the now. It'll be gone soon enough and no one knows what the next hour,much less tomorrow still bring"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="11448932415753590315" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DBg7mfM0yQzJGRKkUDGMgDZaydwi+xE9HS6Sq1DCXjPnHaP9M3sjIhzfeWNHj4eNWv0WO/y9jMvgs0j4VuGW1w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nRLQD76iU4FIoluoG+JP5cUljLRz7YYMSKbj5J/JnJh2F0hrfu25r51kMG8MXEToqYJTU62rG/q1Ozm3mepUfA==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17605567764181654423">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText17605567764181654423" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
